　　手足肉刺　一人手足甲忽然长，倒生肉刺如锥，痛不可忍，吃葵菜自愈。
　　鼻中长毛　一人鼻中出毛，昼夜可长一二尺，渐渐粗圆如绳，痛不可忍，虽忍痛摘去一茎，后即更生。此因食猪羊血过多。遂用乳香、硇砂各一两为末，以饭圆梧桐子大，空心临卧各一服，水下十粒，自然退落。
　　疮如猫眼　一人面上及遍身生疮，似猫儿眼，有光彩，无脓血，但痛痒不常，饮食减少，久则透骨，名曰寒疮。多吃鱼鸡葱韭自愈。
　　肠从胁出　一人胁破肠出，臭秽，急以香油抹肠，用手送入，煎人参枸杞汤服，又淋破处，皮自合矣。吃羊肾粥、赤石脂十日即愈。
　　口鼻黑气　一人口鼻中气出，盘旋不散，凝如黑盖，过十日渐渐至肩胸，与肉相连，坚胜金铁，无由饮食，此多因疟后得之，煎泽兰叶汤，日饮三盏，连服五日愈。[20p]

Thorn-like Flesh on Hands and Feet: A person suddenly had thorn-like growths on their hands and feet, resembling spikes, causing unbearable pain. Eating kale resulted in recovery.

Hairs Growing in the Nose: A person had hairs growing in their nose, which could reach one to two feet in length each day, becoming thick and round like a rope, causing unbearable pain. Although they endured the pain to remove one stalk, it soon regrew. This was due to excessive consumption of pig and sheep's blood. They then used one tael each of myrrh and realgar, powdered, to make pills the size of round cassia seeds. Taking these with water, ten at a time, caused the growths to naturally fall off.

Sores like Cat's Eyes: A person developed sores on their face and body resembling cat's eyes, shining but with no pus or blood, only causing intermittent pain and itchiness, and a decrease in appetite. Over time, it penetrated the bones and was called cold sores. Eating plenty of fish, chicken, scallions, and leeks led to recovery.

Intestines Protruding from the Side: A person had their intestines protruding from their side, foul-smelling. Urgently, fragrant oil was applied to the intestines and pushed back in by hand. A decoction of ginseng and goji berries was consumed, and the broken area was sprinkled with the broth, leading to natural healing. Eating sheep kidney porridge and red resin for ten days resulted in recovery.

Black Gas from Mouth and Nose: A person emitted gas from their mouth and nose, which swirled and did not disperse, forming a black cover. After ten days, it gradually spread to the shoulders and chest, connecting to flesh and becoming harder than gold or iron, making it impossible to eat. This condition arose often after recovering from malaria. Boiling a decoction of marsh lettuce leaves and drinking three cups daily for five consecutive days led to recovery.[20p]

　　肉出如锥　一人遍身忽然肉出如锥，既痒且痛，不能饮食。此名血拥。若不速治，溃而脓出。以赤皮葱烧灰淋洗，吃豉扬数盏，自安。
　　眉动目张　一人眉毛摇动，目不能视，交睫，唤之不应，但能饮食，有经日不效者，用蒜三两取汁，酒调下即愈。
　　毛窍血出　一人毛窍节次血出，若血不出，皮即膨胀如鼓，须臾眼鼻口目俱胀，此名脉溢，饮生姜汁合水各一二盏，即安。
　　伤寒并热　一人忽然气上喘，不能语言，口中汁流吐逆，齿皆摇动，气出转大则闷绝，苏复如是，名曰伤寒并热霍乱。用大黄人参末各半两，水三盏，煎至一盏，去滓热服，可安。
　　口内肉球　一人口内生肉球，臭恶，自己恶见，有根线长五寸余如钗股，吐球出，方可饮食，以手轻捏，痛彻于心，困不可言，用水调生麝香一钱，服数日验。[21p]

Emergence of Flesh Like a Thorn
A person's body suddenly has flesh emerging like a thorn, accompanied by itchiness and pain, making it impossible to eat or drink. This is named "blood engorgement." If not treated promptly, it will ulcerate and discharge pus. Wash it with the ash of red-skinned scallions, and consume a few cups of fermented soybeans for relief.

Eyebrows Moving and Eyes Opening
A person's eyebrows twitch, their eyes unable to see, with crossed eyelashes; they do not respond when called but can eat and drink. If days pass without improvement, take three to six taels of garlic to extract juice and mix it with wine to ingest; this will cure them.

Blood Emergence from Hair Follicles
A person experiences bleeding from their hair follicles in stages, and if there is no blood, the skin will swell like a drum. In a moment, the eyes, nose, and mouth will all swell; this is called "pulse overflow." Drinking a mixture of ginger juice and water, each one or two cups, will bring relief.

Cold Damage and Heat
A person suddenly gasps for breath, unable to speak, with saliva flowing from the mouth and trembling teeth. If the breath becomes labored, they may faint; if revived, the cycle could repeat. This condition is called "cold damage combined with heat and cholera." Use equal parts of rhubarb and ginseng powder, about half a tael each, mixed in three cups of water, boiled down to one cup, strain, and drink hot for relief.

Fleshy Balls in the Mouth
A person develops a foul-smelling fleshy ball in the mouth, which they despise seeing. It has a root-like line over five inches long resembling a hairpin. The ball must be expelled before they can eat or drink. Squeezing it lightly causes intense pain. Use water to mix and take one tael of musk for several days to see results.[21p]

　　泡破石出　一人浑身生燎泡如甘棠梨，每个破出水，内有石一片如指甲大，泡复生，抽尽肌肉，不可治。急用荆三棱、蓬莪朮各五两为末，分三服，酒调连进愈。
　　面热有光　一人头面发热有光色，他人手近之如火烧，用蒜汁半两，酒调下，吐出如蛇状，遂安。
　　离魂假相　一人忽觉自形作两人并卧，不别真假，不语，问亦无对，乃是离魂。用辰砂、人参、茯苓，浓煎汤服之，真者气爽，假者化也。
　　饮酒身瘦　一男子自幼喜饮酒，至成丁后，日饮一二斗不醉，片时无酒，叫呼不绝，全不进食，日就羸弱。其父令用手巾缚住其手足，不令动摇，但扶少立，却取生辣酒一坛，就于其子口边打开，其酒气冲入口中，病者索饮，坚不与之。须臾口中忽吐物一块，直入坛中，即用纸封裹坛口，用猛火烧滚。约酒干一半即开视之，其一块如猪肝样，约三两重，周回有小孔如针眼，不可数计，弃之于江，饮食复旧，虽滴酒不能饮矣。[22p]

A blister breaks, revealing a stone. One person’s whole body is covered in blisters like those of a pear tree; each blister has water inside, with a stone about the size of a fingernail. The blisters recur and consume the flesh, making it untreatable. In urgency, use five taels each of thorny bramble and ground wormwood, and divide into three doses, mixing with wine to intake continuously and recover.

Facial warmth with radiance. One person feels warmth and radiance on their head and face; when others approach, it feels as if they are burning. Use half a tael of garlic juice, mix with wine and administer, allowing them to vomit a snake-like object, resulting in stabilization.

Soul displacement illusion. One person suddenly perceives their being as two people lying together; they cannot distinguish between true and false forms, do not speak, and do not respond when questioned; this is the phenomenon of soul displacement. Use cinnabar, ginseng, and poria, boiling them into a strong decoction to take; the true essence feels refreshed, while the false dissipates.

Drinking causes emaciation. A man has enjoyed drinking since childhood; after reaching adulthood, he drinks one to two dou daily without getting drunk, yet when without wine for a moment, he cries out incessantly and does not eat at all, progressively growing weaker. His father binds his hands and feet with a cloth, preventing movement, only allowing him to stand slightly. Then, he takes a jar of fresh strong wine and opens it near his son’s mouth; the strong aroma rushes into his mouth. The afflicted seeks to drink but is firmly denied. Shortly thereafter, he suddenly vomits a piece into the jar, which is wrapped and sealed with paper, and then set ablaze. After roughly half the wine evaporates, it is opened to reveal a piece resembling pig liver, weighing about three taels, with numerous tiny holes around it, and it cannot be counted. This is discarded into the river, and the person returns to normal eating, although they can no longer drink even a drop of wine.[22p]

　　疮如人面　一商人左髆上有疮如人面，亦无他苦。商人戏滴酒口中，其面亦赤；以物食之，凡物必食。食多觉髆内肉涨起，或不食之，则一臂痹焉。有善医者，教其历试诸药，金石草木悉与之，至贝母，其疮乃聚眉闭口。商人喜曰：此药必治之也。因以小苇筒毁其口灌之，数日成痂遂愈。
　　蛟龙怪病　古有患者，饮食如故，发则如癫，面色青黄，小腹胀满如孕。医者诊其脉，与证皆异，而难明其主疗。忽有一山叟曰：闻开皇六年灞桥有患此病，盖因三月八日水边食芹菜得之。有识者曰：此蛟龙病也。为龙游于芹菜之上，误食而病也。遂以寒食饧每剂五合，服之数服，吐出一物，虽小而似蛟龙状，有两头，其病自此获痊。
　　疮破雀飞　一人左目上睑，忽生一小疮，其形长如鸭卵，其根如弦，恒偃其目不能开。金州防御使崔尧封饮之酒，令大醉，便与割去。疮既破，中有黄雀飞鸣而去。[23p]

A sore like a human face: A merchant had a sore on his left temple that resembled a human face, and it did not cause him much pain. The merchant, when jokingly drinking wine, found his face to also turn red; he had to eat anything that was offered to him. When he ate too much, he felt swelling within his temple, and if he refrained from eating, one of his arms would become numb. A skilled doctor advised him to try various medicines, including metals, stones, herbs, and woods, until he tried Fritillaria, which caused the sore to gather and close. The merchant was pleased and said: "This medicine will surely cure it." He then used a small reed tube to wash it out, and after several days it formed a scab and he was healed.

Strange illness of a dragon: In ancient times, there was a patient who, despite eating and drinking as usual, seemed delirious, his face was green and yellow, and his lower abdomen was swollen as if he were pregnant. The doctor examined his pulse and found that his symptoms did not match any known treatments. Suddenly, an old man from the mountains said: "I heard that in the sixth year of Kaihuang, there was a case of this illness at Baqiao. It was said that it came from eating celery by the water on March 8." A knowledgeable person remarked: "This is the illness of the dragon. It arises because a dragon swam over the celery and was accidentally consumed, leading to the sickness." They then gave him a cold food syrup, five measures per dose, and after several doses he vomited something; although small, it resembled a dragon with two heads, and from then on, he recovered.

A sore breaks and a sparrow flies: A man developed a small sore on the upper eyelid of his left eye that was long like a duck's egg, and its root resembled a string, causing him to keep his eye closed. Cui Yaofeng, the defense commander of Jinzhao, made him drink wine until he was very drunk and then helped to cut it off. Once the sore was broken, a yellow sparrow flew out and chirped as it departed.[23p]

　　身渐缩小　世有奇疾，终莫能晓。昔吕缙叔以制诰知颍州，忽得疾，身体日渐缩小，人不能医。临终，仅如小儿。古人不曾患此疾，终无人识。
　　视物倒植　元末四明吕复别号沧洲，翁深于医道，临川道士萧云泉眼中视物皆倒植，请复治。问其因，曰：某尝大醉，尽吐所饮酒，熟睡至天明，遂得此病。复诊其脉，左关浮促，即告之曰：伤酒大吐，上焦反复，致倒其胆腑，故视物皆倒植，不内外因。法当复吐以正其胆。遂用藜芦、瓜蒂为粗末，水煎，使平旦顿服，以吐为度。吐毕，视物如常。
　　视直如曲　一妇人视物如曲弓，视界尺之直亦如曲钩，药莫能治。
　　呕物如舌　镇阳有士人嗜酒，日饮数斗，饮兴一发则不遏。一夕大醉，呕出一物，如舌，初视无痕窍，至欲饮时，眼遍其上，矗然而起，家人沃之以酒立尽，至常日所饮之数而止。遂投之猛火，自出裂为十数片。士人自此恶酒不饮。[24p]

The body gradually shrinks; there is a strange illness that ultimately no one can comprehend. In the past, Lu Jinshu was appointed to govern Yingzhou. Suddenly, he fell ill, and his body shrank day by day, becoming unhealable. At his end, he was as small as a child. The ancients had never suffered from this illness, and thus no one recognized it.

Regarding the inverted vision, during the late Yuan dynasty, Lu Fubei of Siming, also known as Cangzhou, was deeply knowledgeable in medicine. The Taoist Xiaoyunquan of Linchuan reported that he saw objects as inverted and asked for treatment. When asked about the cause, he said: "I once got extremely drunk and vomited all the wine I drank. I slept soundly until dawn, and from then on, I acquired this illness." Upon examining his pulse, it was floating and rapid on the left side. He was told: "Alcohol consumption and excessive vomiting have caused a reversal in your upper organs, leading to the distortion of your gallbladder, which is why you see everything inverted; it is not due to internal or external factors. The treatment should be to expel it again to correct your gallbladder." Hence, he used coarse powder made from donkeys’ gall and gourd seeds, boiled in water, and instructed to take it first thing in the morning, to induce vomiting as necessary. After the vomiting, his vision returned to normal.

As for the woman who saw objects as if they were bent like a bow, she perceived straight lines as if they were curved hooks, and no medicine could cure her.

In Zhenyang, there was a scholar who was fond of drinking, consuming several dou each day, and when the urge struck, he could not be restrained. One evening, in a state of great intoxication, he vomited something that resembled a tongue. At first glance, it seemed without any openings or marks, but as he wished to drink, it stood upright. His family poured wine over it until nothing remained, stopping only when they reached the daily amount he usually drank. They then threw it into a fierce fire, where it split into several pieces. From that point on, the scholar could no longer tolerate alcohol.[24p]

　　病消食龙　《齐谐记》云：江夏郡安陆县隆安中有郭坦兄弟三人，大兄得天行病后，遂大能食，一日食斗米，其家给五年贫罄，后乞食至一家门前，已得饭，又复乞其后门。其家人怒之云：前门已饭了，又从后门来讨，那得许多与你？彼答云：腹中饥甚，实不知是后门。门园有薤三畦，彼就地而啖其二。须臾闷卧在地，大吐一物如龙，因出渐渐小，人持饭与，遂不复食，将饭着所吐之物上，即消化成水，此病寻瘥。
　　妇人异疾　一妇异疾，每腹胀则腹中有声如击鼓，远闻于外。人行过其门者，皆疑其家作乐。腹胀消则鼓声亦止，一月一作，经百医皆莫能明其疾。
　　腹内钟鸣　有妊妇腹内如钟鸣，一贫士用鼠窟前畚土研罗为末，每服二钱，麝香汤调服，其疾即愈。[25p]

The Illness of the Gluttonous Dragon

In "Records of Qi and Harmony," it is said that in Long'an County, Anlu Prefecture, there were three brothers named Guo Tan. The eldest brother, after contracting the celestial illness, was able to eat greatly; in one day, he consumed an entire dou of rice. His family suffered from poverty for five years, and eventually, he had to beg for food. One day, he reached a house where he had already received rice at the front door but then went around to the back to beg again.

The family, angry, said, "You’ve already received food at the front; how can we give you more at the back?" He replied, "I am extremely hungry and truly did not realize it was the back door." In the garden, there were three beds of garlic leeks, and he ate two of them on the spot. Soon, he lay down on the ground in distress and vomited something resembling a dragon. As it came out, it gradually shrunk in size. When people brought him rice, he no longer wanted to eat. They placed the rice on the thing he had vomited, which quickly turned into water, and this illness was soon cured.

A Woman with a Strange Illness

There was a woman who suffered from a peculiar ailment: whenever her abdomen swelled, there would be a sound inside her like a drum, audible from outside. Those who passed by her door would often suspect that her family was celebrating. When the swelling in her abdomen went down, the drum sound would cease. This happened once a month for an entire year, and despite consulting a hundred doctors, no one could diagnose her condition.

The Bell Sound in the Abdomen

There was a pregnant woman whose abdomen sounded like a bell. A poor scholar ground earth from a rat's burrow into powder and mixed it with two qian of musk broth. After taking this mixture, her ailment was cured.[25p]

　　产妇腹痒　箭簳及镞，主治妇人产后腹中痒，安所卧床席下，勿令人知。
　　产后肠痒　针线袋，主治妇人产后肠中痒不可忍，以袋安所卧褥下，勿令人知。
　　杯中蛇影　陈留何解元一日饮于赵修武宅，酒至，陈忽见杯中似有小蛇，入口亦不觉有物，但每思而疑之，日久觉心痛，自思蛇入腹，为患不浅。后复会其宅，恰才执杯，又见小蛇，乃放杯细看，乃粱上挂弓一张，蛇影乃弓梢之影是也。遂解其疑，痛即止。
　　食挂　眉州米思古得疾，不能食，闻荤腥则呕，惟用大铛旋煮汤沃淡饭数数食之，医莫能治。史载之曰：俗辈不读《内经》而妄医人之疾，可叹可骇！君之疾，正在《素问》经中，名曰食挂。凡人之肺六叶，舒张而盖下，覆于脾，子母气和则进食。一或有戾则肺不能舒，脾之为弊，故不嗜食。遂授一方，以清气润肺为治，服三日，病者鼻闻肉味觉香，取啖之甚美。此宋人载于传记，考之《素问》，并无食挂之病，或记者假托耳。[26p]

  • Postpartum Abdominal Itch: For women experiencing itching in the abdomen after giving birth, use an arrowhead and a flint, placing it under the bed mat. Do not let anyone know.

  • Postpartum Intestinal Itch: For women experiencing unbearable itching in the intestines after giving birth, use a needle and thread bag, placing it under the bedding. Do not let anyone know.

  • Cups and the Shadow of a Snake: One day, Chen Liu Hejie drank at the residence of Zhao Xiuwu. As the wine was served, Chen suddenly saw a small snake in the cup. He felt nothing enter but was troubled by this thought, leading to heart pain over time, believing a snake had entered his abdomen and posed a serious threat. Later, when he returned to that residence and picked up the cup again, he saw the small snake again. He then examined the cup closely and realized it was actually the shadow of a bow hanging from the millet above. This revelation relieved his doubt, and the pain ceased.

  • Food Hanging: In Meizhou, a man named Si Gu fell ill and could not eat, feeling nauseous at the smell of meat. He could only consume rice washed with soup prepared in a large pot. Despite various doctors attempting to treat him, none succeeded. Historical records state: it is lamentable and terrifying that the common folk practice medicine without studying the "Inner Canon"! Your illness is recorded in the "Suwen" as "food hanging." The human lungs are made up of six lobes, which expand and cover the spleen. When the maternal and child energies are in harmony, one can eat. If any disturbance occurs, the lungs cannot expand, leading to spleen dysfunction and lack of appetite. A prescription was provided to clear the energy and moisten the lungs. After three days of treatment, the patient smelled the aroma of meat and found it delicious. This was recorded by a Song dynasty writer, but upon review of the "Suwen," no such ailment as "food hanging" is mentioned, suggesting a misattribution by the journalist.[26p]

　　毛如铁条　一白人忽变黑，毛直如铁条，虽饮食，不语如大醉，名无血钻。
　　眼见五色　一人酒色过度，眼见空中有五色物，稍近变成一美妇人，亭亭而立。徐之才曰：此色欲多，大虚所致，乃处补药饮之，数剂而愈。
　　面肿如蛇　一人头面肉肿如蛇状，用湿砖上青苔一钱，水调涂立消。
　　遍身赤肉　有小儿初生，遍身无皮，俱是赤肉，掘土坑卧一宿，即长皮。又方：用白早米粉干扑于上，候生皮乃止。
　　脑窍　一妇人年少，脑生一窍，凡咳脓血，与窍相应而出，此肺痿也，用参、芪、归、芍，加退热排脓之剂而愈。[27p]

  • Hair like iron bars: A white person suddenly turned black, with hair straight like iron bars. Despite eating and drinking, they did not speak, appearing as if deeply intoxicated. This condition is called "blood diamond without blood."

  • Seeing five colors: A person excessively indulged in wine and pleasure saw five-colored objects in the air. As they got closer, it transformed into a beautiful woman, standing gracefully. Xu Zhicao said: This is caused by excessive desires and great emptiness. It can be treated with restorative medicines; a few doses will lead to recovery.

  • Face swollen like a snake: A person had facial swelling resembling a snake. Using a wet brick topped with green moss and adjusting it with water, the condition can be alleviated immediately.

  • Whole body without skin: A newborn child was born without skin, with the whole body covered in red flesh. By digging a pit in the ground and sleeping there for a night, the skin will grow. Alternatively, use white rice flour to powder the body until the skin forms.

  • Brain orifice: A young woman had an orifice in her brain, and whenever she coughed up pus and blood, it corresponded with the orifice. This is called pulmonary phthisis; it can be treated with ginseng, astragalus, angelica, and white peony, along with medicines to reduce fever and expel pus for recovery.[27p]

　　胞满　一妇产后有伤，胞破不能小便，常常渗漏不干，用生丝绢一片剪碎，白牡丹根皮、白芨末各一钱，水一碗，煎至绢烂如饧，空心顿服，不可声言，即效。
　　蛇头疮　患疮如蛇头，突出数寸，用雄黄、硫黄涂之，即消。
　　心疾见狮　有患心疾，见物如狮子，程伊川教以手直前捕之，见其无物，久久自愈。
　　观壁皆莲　一妇病热，目视壁上皆是红莲花，医用滚痰丸下之愈。
　　乳悬　妇产后，忽然两乳细小下垂，痛甚，名曰乳悬。用芎、归各二斤，内用半斤煎水服，余以烧烟熏口鼻，二料乃愈。
　　水道出线　一妇产后，水道中出肉线一条，长尺余，动之则痛欲绝。先服失笑散数服，次以带皮姜三斤研烂，入清油二斤，煎干为度，用绢兜起肉线，屈曲于水道边，以煎姜熏之，冷则熨之，一日夜缩其大半，二日则尽。又再服失笑散、芎归汤调理。如肉线断，不可治。[28p]

Abdominal Swelling: A woman experiences injury after giving birth, with her abdomen bloated and unable to urinate, often leaking continuously. Take a piece of raw silk, cut it into small fragments, and combine it with one coin each of white peony root and white atractylodes powder, boiling it in a bowl of water until the silk disintegrates like syrup. Take it on an empty stomach without speaking, and it will be effective.

Snake-like Ulcer: If there is an ulcer resembling a snake’s head, protruding several inches, apply realgar and sulfur to it, and it will diminish.

Heart Disease with Lion Vision: A person suffering from heart disease sees objects as lions. Cheng Yichuan teaches to extend the hand forward as if to catch it. Upon seeing nothing, he slowly recovers.

Lotus Appearance on the Wall: A woman suffering from heat sees red lotus flowers on the wall. The doctor uses rolling phlegm pills to treat her, and she is cured.

Suspended Breast: After childbirth, a woman suddenly has small, drooping, and painful breasts, termed "suspended breast." Use two jin each of chuanxiong and angelica, boil half a jin in water and take it. The rest should be burned to create smoke for inhalation, both ingredients will lead to recovery.

Flesh Line from the Water Passage: After childbirth, a woman has a flesh line protruding from her water passage, over a foot long, causing extreme pain if moved. First, take several doses of Shixiao Powder, then grind three jin of ginger with the skin, mix it with two jin of clear oil, and boil it down. Use silk to wrap the flesh line and bend it near the water passage, applying steam from the boiled ginger, and when it cools, apply heat. Within a day and night, it will reduce by more than half, and it will completely resolve in two days. Also, take additional doses of Shixiao Powder and a chuanxiong-angelica decoction to regulate. If the flesh line breaks, it cannot be treated.[28p]

　　灸火出血　有人灸火至五壮，血出一缕，急如溺，手冷欲绝，以酒炒黄芩一二钱为末，酒下止。
　　头皮蛆出　一人头皮内时有蛆出，以刀切破皮，用丝瓜叶捣汁搽之，蛆出尽，根绝。
　　痘烂生蛆　小儿痘烂生蛆，以柳条带叶铺地，将儿卧其上，蛆尽出而愈。
　　疮孔儿啼　一人渊疽发于肋下，久则溃窍，有声如儿啼，灸阳陵泉二七壮即止。
　　指节断落　有人手指节间痛不可忍，渐至断落，以蓖麻子去壳二两，碎者不用，黄连四两，贮瓶内，水二升浸之，春夏三日，秋冬五日，每早向东以此水吞下蓖麻子一粒，渐加至四五粒。微泄无害。忌食动风物，屡验。
　　耳内雀声　一人患头风证，耳内常鸣，如鸟雀啾唧之声，此挟脑风火之声也，用川当归煎服而愈。[29p]

  • Burning with Blood Loss: A person suffered a burn with blood loss to the extent of a thread. It was urgent like a need to urinate, and their hands were cold and almost lifeless. Grind one or two qian of roasted Huangqin into a powder and take it with wine to stop the bleeding.

  • Maggots Emerging from the Scalp: One person had maggots emerging from their scalp. They cut open the skin with a knife and applied juice from loofah leaves, leading to the complete expulsion of the maggots and their eradication.

  • Pox Decaying and Infested with Maggots: A child had pox that decayed and produced maggots. They laid the child on the ground covered with willow branches and leaves, resulting in the complete expulsion of the maggots and recovery.

  • Cry of a Child from an Ulcer Opening: A person had a deep sore under the rib, which eventually burst, making a sound resembling a child's cry. They cauterized the Yanglingquan point with seven strong burns, which immediately stopped.

  • Knuckle Pain Leading to Detachment: A person had unbearable pain between their finger joints, gradually leading to detachment. Take two liang of shelled castor seeds (discarding crushed ones), and four liang of Huanglian. Put them in a bottle with two sheng of water to soak—three days in spring and summer, five days in autumn and winter. Every morning, swallow one castor seed with this water facing east, gradually increasing to four to five seeds. A slight release is harmless. Avoid eating foods that stir up wind conditions, as proven repeatedly.

  • Sounds of Sparrows in the Ear: One person suffering from head wind syndrome experienced constant ringing in the ear, resembling the chirping of sparrows. This was a sign of wind-heat in the brain. Taking a decoction of Sichuan Donggui cured it.[29p]

　　伤寒舌出　一人伤寒，舌出寸余，连日不收。用梅花、冰片搽舌上，应手而收，重者用三钱方愈。
　　产后舌出　妇人产后，舌出不能收，以朱砂傅其舌，令作产儿之状，以一女扶之，壁外潜将瓦器忽然崩坠响声，妇闻而惊，舌则收。
　　产子母虫　一妇人忽产虫一对，在地上能行，长寸余，自后月生一对。以苦参加杀虫药为丸服之，又生一对埋于土中，过数日发而视之，大如拳，名子母虫，从此绝根。
　　眼中出血　一妇人眼中血如射而出，或沿鼻流下，但出血多时，即经不行，乃阴虚相火之病。遂用当归、生地、酒芍，加柴胡、黄连、黄蘗、知母、条芩、侧柏、木通、桃仁、红花，水煎，食前服愈。
　　你头开裂　你头开裂，用秋后嫩茄子裂开头者，阴干烧为末，水调服。
　　遍身红点　男子每至秋冬，遍身发红点作痒，此寒气收敛，腠理阳气不能发越，怫郁内作也，宜用人参败毒散解表，再用补中益气汤实表而愈。[30p]

Scarlet Fever with Protruding Tongue: A person with scarlet fever has a tongue protruding over an inch for several consecutive days without retracting. Apply plum blossom and borneol to the tongue; it will retract immediately. For severe cases, use three cents (a weight measure) to cure it.

Protruding Tongue After Childbirth: A woman after childbirth has a tongue that cannot retract. Apply cinnabar to the tongue, making it resemble the shape of a newborn, and have a girl support her. Outside the wall, suddenly drop a瓦器 (earthen vessel) to create a loud noise, which will startle the woman and cause her tongue to retract.

Mother Worm After Giving Birth: A woman gives birth to a pair of worms that can move on the ground, each over an inch long. After a month, a new pair is born. Mix bitter herbs with insecticidal medicine to form pills for oral ingestion. If another pair appears and is buried in the ground, after several days, they will grow as large as a fist, known as 'mother worms', and from then on, they will be eradicated.

Blood in the Eyes: A woman has blood shooting out from her eyes, sometimes flowing down her nose. If there is a lot of bleeding, menstruation stops, which indicates a deficiency of Yin and an excess of fire. Consequently, use angelica, raw rehmannia, liquorice, add chaihu, huanglian, huangbai, zhimu, qinghao, cedar, moutan, and red flower, boil them in water, and take before meals for recovery.

Split Head: For a split head, take tender eggplant after autumn, split it, dry it in the shade, burn it into a powder, and mix with water to ingest.

Red Dots All Over the Body: A man presents with red dots all over his body that become itchy each autumn and winter. This is due to the cold air condensing, preventing Yang Qi from surfacing, causing internal stagnation. It is advisable to use Ren Shen Bai Du San to release the exterior, and then use Bu Zhong Yi Qi Tang to strengthen the exterior for recovery.[30p]

　　遍身紫泡　一人因剥死牛，瞀闷，遍身俱发紫泡，闷绝，便急刺破泡，良久遂收而苏醒，更与败毒药愈。
　　红丝瘤　一人间东垣曰：某生一子，一岁后，生红丝瘤而死。后生四子皆然，何也？曰：汝乃肾中伏火，精乃有红丝故也，俗名胎瘤。汝试以精验之，果然。令服滋肾丸，其妻服六味地黄丸，后受胎生子，前证不作。
　　产后食茶　一妇人产后，日食茶二十余碗，一月后遍身冰冷数块，人以指按其冷处即从指下上应至心，如是者二年，诸医不效。以八物汤去地黄加橘红，入姜汁竹沥一酒杯，十服而温。
　　闻雷昏倒　一小儿七岁，闻雷即昏倒。以人参、当归身、麦门冬，少入五味子，熬膏，尽剂后，闻雷自若。
　　别有一喉　一人但饮食若别有一喉咙斜过膈下，径达左胁而作痞闷，以手按之，则沥沥有声，以控涎丹十粒服之，少时痞处热作，一声转泻下痰饮二升，再饮食，正下而达胃矣。[31p]

  1. Purple Blisters: A man who skinned a cow became distressed and developed purple blisters all over his body. He was in grave agony, so he urgently stabbed the blisters. After a long time, he managed to recover and was treated with antidote drugs.

  2. Red Silk Tumor: A person in the eastern courtyard said: "I had a son, and after one year, he developed a red silk tumor and died. Later, all four of my sons had the same condition. What is the cause?" The reply was: "You have a hidden fire in your kidneys, and the essence has red silks due to this, commonly known as fetal tumors. You should test it with essence, and it will be confirmed. Take kidney-replenishing pills, while your wife should take the Six-Flavor Rehmannia Pill. Afterward, she will conceive and bear children without previous issues."

  3. Postpartum Tea Consumption: A woman, after giving birth, consumed more than twenty bowls of tea daily. A month later, she had patches of ice-coldness all over her body; if someone pressed a cold spot with a finger, it would resonate up to her heart. This continued for two years with no effectiveness from various doctors. Using an Eight-Ingredient Decoction, minus the rehmannia, and adding tangerine peel, along with a cup of ginger juice and bamboo sap, she took it ten times and felt warmth.

  4. Fainting at Thunder: A seven-year-old child fainted upon hearing thunder. After using ginseng, Angelica sinensis, and Ophiopogon, with a little Schisandra added, a syrup was prepared. After finishing the medicine, he became unaffected by thunder.

  5. A Throat Like Another: A person felt as though there was another throat that passed obliquely below the diaphragm, reaching directly to the left side, causing a sensation of fullness and heaviness. When pressed, a dripping sound could be heard. After taking ten pills of a saliva-regulating elixir, after a short time, the heaviness turned to heat, leading to a discharge of phlegm of about two liters. After resuming food, it properly descended and reached the stomach.[31p]

　　三阴交血出　一妇三阴交无故血出如射，将绝，以指按其窍，缚以布条，昏倒不知人。以人参一两煎汤灌之，愈。
　　项肿与头相统　一人颈项肿，与头相统，按之坚硬，漏芦汤一剂，服下发痒，顷刻消散。
　　痒入骨髓　一人田间收稻，忽然遍身痒入骨髓，此痰气也。用食盐九钱，泡汤三碗，每进一碗，探而吐之，三进三探，则不痒矣。
　　产户一物如泡　丹溪治一妇产户下一物如泡有尖，约重斤余，却喜血不尽虚，急与黄芪、白朮、升麻各五分，人参、当归各一钱，水煎，连服三剂即收愈。
　　胸间溃窍　一少妇胸溃一窍，有脓血，与口中所咳相应而出。以参、芪、当归，加退热排脓等药而愈。
　　玉茎长肿　一少年玉茎挺长，肿而痿，皮塌常润，磨股难行，两腿气冲上，手足倦弱。先以小柴胡汤加黄连，大剂行其湿热，少加黄蘗降其逆上之气，肿渐消，茎中硬块未尽；以青皮为君，佐以散风之药为末服，外以丝瓜汁调五倍子傅之，愈。[32p]

  • Three Yin Intersection Bleeding: A woman experienced unexplained bleeding at the Three Yin Intersection, as if it were shooting out. She was close to fainting, so her acupoint was pressed with a finger and bound with a cloth strip. She fell unconscious. After administering a decoction of one tael of ginseng, she recovered.

  • Neck Swelling Connected to the Head: A man had swelling in the neck that was connected to the head, and it felt hard upon palpation. After taking a decoction of Luoluo (a type of herb), he experienced itching, and shortly after, the swelling dissipated.

  • Itching to the Bone Marrow: A person harvesting rice in the fields suddenly experienced itching all over as if it reached the bone marrow. This was due to phlegm and qi. Nine qian of table salt was used to soak in three bowls of water; with each bowl consumed, he would probe and vomit it out. After three bouts of this, he was no longer itchy.

  • A Bulbous Growth from Childbirth: Danxi treated a woman with a bulbous growth under the childbirth portal that was pointed and weighed about a jin. The bleeding was excessive yet weak. She was urgently given five fen each of astragalus, baizhu, and shengma, and one qian each of ginseng and angelica, decocted in water. After taking three doses, she was cured.

  • Ulcer in the Chest: A young woman had an ulcer in her chest that was producing pus and blood, correlating with what she coughed up. Treatment included ginseng, astragalus, and angelica, along with medications to reduce heat and drain pus, leading to recovery.

  • Swelling of the Penile Shaft: A young man had an elongated swelling on the penile shaft, which was soft and moistened with a drooping appearance, making movement difficult. Both legs felt congested upwards, and he experienced weakness in the limbs. Initially, he was given a small dose of Chai Hu Decoction with added Huanglian to reduce damp heat, and a small amount of Huangbo to lower the rebellious qi. The swelling gradually reduced, but hardened nodules remained in the shaft. He was treated with Qingpi as the main ingredient, combined with medicinal powders to disperse wind, and externally applied a mixture of silk gourd juice with wuzhuyu, resulting in recovery.[32p]

　　阴茎肿大　一人茎头肿大如升，光如鱼泡，以二陈汤加升麻、青黛、牡蛎，水煎服二剂。愈。
　　阴户如石　一妇产后，因子死，经断不行半年。一日小腹忽痛，阴户内有物如石硬塞之而痛不禁。群医不识。青林曰：此石瘕也。用四物汤加桃仁、大黄、三棱、槟榔、延胡索、附子、泽泻、血竭为汤，二剂而愈。
　　疮血如溺　一人左手无名指爪角生一小疮，初起麻粒大，用小刀挑开疮头，血出如溺不止。一日夜长出肉瘤如菌，裹指顶，内开一孔，如眼目转动，此疔毒也。以艾灸四十壮，不知疼痒，后烙之，剪去肉瘤，傅收疔散，外以膏药贴之，内服解毒汤，七日愈。
　　皮生恶物　一女十六岁，四肢软皮处生恶物如黄豆大，半在肉内，红紫色痛甚，诸药不效。方士教买水银四两，以白纸二张揉熟，蘸水银擦三日，自落而愈。[33p]

  • Enlarged Penis: A person had an enlarged penis tip that was swollen like a mound, translucent like a fish bladder. A decoction was made with Erchen Decoction, adding Shengma, Qingdai, and Oyster. After taking two doses, he recovered.

  • Hardened Vulva: After giving birth, a woman lost her child and had no menstruation for six months. One day she suddenly experienced abdominal pain, with something hard like a stone blocking her vulva, causing unbearable pain. Many doctors could not identify the issue. Qinglin said: This is a stone mass. A decoction was made from Siwu Decoction, adding Tao Ren, Dahuang, Sanling, Binglang, Yan Hu Suo, Fuzi, Zexie, and Xuejie. After two doses, she recovered.

  • Blood Like Urine: A person had a small sore at the tip of their left ring finger, initially the size of a grain. After pricking it with a small knife, blood flowed out continuously like urine. One night, a fleshy lump like a fungus grew on the tip, forming a small opening that moved like an eye. This was a case of carbuncle. He was treated with moxibustion for forty applications without feeling pain or itch; subsequently, it was cauterized, and the lump was cut off. A topical herbal salve was applied, and an internal detoxification decoction was taken. He recovered in seven days.

  • Malignant Growth on Skin: A sixteen-year-old girl had malignant growths the size of soybeans on the soft skin of her limbs, half embedded in the flesh, reddish-purple and very painful. Various medications were ineffective. A practitioner advised her to purchase four ounces of mercury, rubbing it on with two sheets of white paper for three days until it fell off, leading to her recovery.[33p]

　　胆衡　一产妇因事大恐而病，病虽愈，惟目张不闭。人皆不能晓，问于钱仲阳曰：病名胆衡。煮(木郁)李仁酒饮之，使醉即愈。所以然者，目系内连肝胆，恐则气结，胆衡不下，(木郁)李仁可去结，随酒入胆，结去胆下，目则能闭矣。如言而效。
　　腹内虾(虫麻)　汾州王氏病右胁有声如虾(虫麻)，常欲手按之，否则声声相接。医不能辨。留阳山人赵峦诊之曰：此因惊气入于脏腑而成。与镇惊朱砂丸，以虾(虫麻)衣汤送下，遂瘥。虾(虫麻)衣，即车前草也。
　　　诸虫门

　　　　黄帝素问

　　　　　气交变大论

　　岁木不及，收杀气行，寒雨害物，虫食甘黄，脾土受邪。　　 【注　夏秋之交，土气用事，而反为寒雨所胜故也。】　　岁土不及，复则收政严峻，名木苍雕，虫食甘黄，气客于脾。　　 【注　气，水气也。虫食甘黄，气客于脾，水浸土也。】[34p]

Gall Bladder Disorder
A woman in labor became extremely frightened and fell ill. Although she recovered, her eyes remained wide open and could not close. No one could understand the issue, so they asked Qian Zhongyang who diagnosed it as a gall bladder disorder. He advised them to brew a drink with the kernels of the (mu yu) plum and give it to her until she became intoxicated, which would cure her. The reason for this is that the eyes are internally connected to the liver and gall bladder, and fear causes energy to become stagnant, preventing the gall bladder from descending. The (mu yu) plum kernels can alleviate the stagnation, entering the gall bladder along with the wine, allowing the stagnation to be relieved so that the eyes can then close. The treatment worked as described.

Insect Sounds in the Abdomen
Wang from Fen Zhou experienced a sound in his right side that resembled the sound of shrimp, and he often felt the need to press it, otherwise the sounds would repeat endlessly. The doctors could not discern what was wrong. Zhao Luan, a man from Liu Yang Mountain, diagnosed it as caused by fright causing qi to enter the organs. He provided a calming remedy, the Zhenshijing Zhu Shawan, which was taken with a soup made with the skin of the shrimp, and he subsequently healed. The skin of the shrimp refers to plantago.

Discussion of Insects

Yellow Emperor's Sutra

Essentials of Qi and Seasonal Changes
In a year when wood fails to grow, malevolent energy circulates, cold rain harms the plants, and insects consume the sweet yellow, leading to an affliction of the spleen earth. [Note: This occurs during the transition between summer and autumn when earth energy is predominant, but is overcome by cold rain.] In a year when earth fails to thrive, the governance becomes strict, the wood is dark and moldy, insects consume the sweet yellow, and qi is entrapped in the spleen. [Note: Here, qi refers to water vapor. Insects consume the sweet yellow, and qi is trapped in the spleen, due to water saturating the earth.][34p]

　　　　灵枢经

　　　　　邪气脏腑病形篇

　　脾脉微滑为虫毒，蛔蝎腹热。
　　 【注　脾为湿阴之土，滑为湿热之脉，湿热则生虫也。】
　　　　　五癃津液别篇

　　中热则胃中消谷，消谷则虫上下作，肠胃充郭故胃缓；胃缓则气逆，故唾出。　　 【注　胃缓，则少阴之气不与阳明相合，反上逆于廉泉，则水液随之，故涎唾也。】
　　　　　上膈篇

　　气为上膈者，食饮入而还出，虫为下膈。下膈者，食晬时乃出。　　 【注　上膈者，上焦之气也。下膈者，中焦之气也。】
　　　　　论疾诊尺篇

　　肘后粗以下三四寸热者，肠中有虫。
　　　　金匮要略 【汉　张机】

　　　　　狐惑

　　狐惑之为病，状如伤寒，默默欲眠，目不得闭，卧起不安，蚀于喉为惑，蚀于阴为狐，不欲饮食，恶闻食臭，其面目乍赤、乍黑、乍白，蚀于上部则声嗄，甘草泻心汤主之。　　蚀于下部则咽干，苦参汤洗之。[35p]

Spiritual Pivot Classic

On the Symptoms of Diseases Related to Pathogenic Factors Affecting Organs

The spleen meridian is slightly slippery, indicating worm toxins, such as in cases of heat from ascaris or scorpions in the abdomen.
[Note: The spleen is the wet, yin aspect of the earth; slipping indicates a moist and hot meridian, which gives rise to worms.]

On the Separateness of Fluids in Five Lin Diseases

When there is heat in the middle, the stomach loses its ability to digest grains; with the grains undigested, worms cause disturbances up and down, hence the stomach feels full and relaxed; if the stomach is relaxed, qi reverses, leading to the expulsion of saliva.
[Note: If the stomach is relaxed, the lesser yin qi does not join with the greater yang, causing it to reverse and bring water fluids along, hence saliva and drool are produced.]

On the Upper Partition

The qi of the upper partition allows food and drink to enter and then exit; the worms are at the lower partition. The lower partition only expels food remnants at the proper time.
[Note: The upper partition refers to the qi of the upper jiao; the lower partition refers to the qi of the middle jiao.]

On Diagnosing Illness by Pulse Measurement

If the pulse in the area three to four inches below the elbow feels hot, it indicates the presence of worms in the intestines.

From the Golden Chamber Essentials
(Han Dynasty, Zhang Ji)

Hound Illness

The illness of hound is characterized by a presentation similar to that of a cold. The patient desires to sleep silently but cannot close their eyes, feels restless in lying and rising, experiences erosion in the throat indicating disturbance, is affected in the lower regions indicating a hound spirit, has no desire for food and aversion to the smell of food, and their complexion may appear red, black, or pale; if the upper region is affected, there is hoarseness, treated with Licorice Heart Decoct; if the lower region is affected, there is a dry throat, treated with bitter herb decoction.[35p]

　　蚀于肛者，雄黄熏之。

　　　　千金方 【唐　孙思邈】

　　　　　九虫

　　夫人腹中有尸虫，此物与人俱生，而为人大害。尸虫之形状似大马尾，或如薄筋，依脾而居，乃有头尾，皆长三寸。又有九虫：一曰伏虫，长四分；二曰蛔虫，长一尺；三曰白虫，长一寸；四曰肉虫，状如烂杏；五曰肺虫，状如蚕；六曰胃虫，状如虾蟆；七曰弱虫，状如瓜瓣；八曰赤虫，状如生肉；九曰蛲虫，至细微，形如菜虫状。伏虫则群虫之主也；蛔虫贯心杀人；白虫相生，子孙转多，其母转大，长至四五寸，亦能杀人；肉虫令人烦满；肺虫令人欬嗽；胃虫令人呕吐，胃逆喜哕；弱虫又名膈虫，令人多唾；赤虫令人肠鸣；蛲虫居胴肠之间，多则为痔，剧则为癞。因人疮痍，即生诸痈疽、癣瘘、瘑疥。龋虫无所不为，人亦不必尽有，有亦不必尽多，或偏有，或偏无，类妇人常多，其虫凶恶，人之极患也。常以白筵草沐浴佳，根叶皆可用。既是香草，且是尸虫所畏也。[36p]

For those afflicted in the rectum, the remedy is to fumigate with realgar.

"Thousand Gold Prescriptions" by Sun Simiao, Tang Dynasty

The Nine Worms

When there are corpse worms in a woman's abdomen, they are born with the individual and can cause severe harm. The corpse worm resembles a large horse tail or thin tendons, residing in the spleen, with a front and rear, each about three inches long. There are also nine kinds of worms:

  1. The Fuzhong worm, four-tenths of a foot long;
  2. The Ascaris, one foot long;
  3. The White worm, one inch long;
  4. The Flesh worm, resembling a rotten apricot;
  5. The Lung worm, resembling a silkworm;
  6. The Stomach worm, resembling a frog;
  7. The Weak worm, resembling melon seeds;
  8. The Red worm, resembling raw meat;
  9. The Pin worm, very small, resembling a caterpillar.

The Fuzhong worm is the leader among the worms; the Ascaris can penetrate the heart and kill; the White worm reproduces quickly, with many offspring, causing the mother to grow large, reaching four or five inches, also capable of causing death; the Flesh worm leads to discomfort; the Lung worm causes coughing; the Stomach worm induces vomiting, with upward gastric reflux; the Weak worm, also known as the diaphragm worm, causes excessive salivation; the Red worm leads to intestinal noises; the Pin worm resides in the intestines, and when numerous, can result in hemorrhoids, severe cases causing sores and scabs.

Tooth worms do everything harmful; individuals need not have them all, nor in abundance; some may have them, others may not, often women have many. These worms are ferocious and are a great affliction to humans. It is recommended to bathe with white yarrow, as both its roots and leaves are useful. Not only is it a fragrant herb, but it is also feared by the corpse worms.[36p]

　　凡欲服补药及治诸病，皆须去诸虫并痰饮宿癖除尽，方可服补药，不尔必不得药力。　　凡得伤寒及天行热病，腹中有热，又人食少，肠胃空虚，三虫行作求食，蚀人五脏及下部。若齿龂无色，舌上尽白，甚者唇里有疮，四肢沉重，忽忽善眠。当数看其上唇内有疮唾血，唇内如栗疮者，心内懊憹痛闷，此虫在上，蚀其五脏；下唇内生疮者，其人喜眠，此虫在下，蚀其下部，人不能知。可服此蚀虫药，不尔，(上匿下虫)虫杀人。又曰：凡患湿(上匿下虫)者，多是热病后，或久下痢不止，或有客热结在腹中，或易水土温凉气着，多生此病。亦有干(上匿下虫)，不甚泄痢而下部疮痒，不问干湿，久则杀人。凡湿得冷而苦痢，单煮黄连及艾叶、苦参之属，皆可用之。若病人齿龂无色，舌上白者，或喜眠烦愦，不知痛痒处，或下痢，急治下部。不晓此者，但攻其上，不以下部为意，下部生虫，虫蚀其肛，肛烂见五脏便死，烧艾于竹筒熏之。[37p]

In general, anyone wishing to take tonics or treat various diseases must first eliminate all parasites and phlegm and resolve lingering issues; only then can one take tonics, as otherwise the medicinal effects will not be achieved.

For those suffering from cold damage or epidemic fever, if there is heat in the abdomen and the person eats little, leading to emptiness in the stomach and intestines, the three parasites will seek food, eroding the five internal organs and lower parts. If there is no color around the gums, and the tongue is entirely white, in severe cases, there may be sores inside the lips, heaviness in the limbs, and an inclination to sleep. One should examine the inside of the upper lip for sores and spitting blood, and if there are sores inside the lower lip, this indicates that the parasites in the upper part erode the internal organs, while those in the lower part lead to excessive sleepiness—these parasites are often unnoticed.

One may take medicines to eradicate these parasites; otherwise, the hidden parasites can be deadly. Additionally, those suffering from moisture-related issues (with upper parasites hidden and lower parasites present) often have them arise after heat illness, prolonged diarrhea, or from external factors like warm, humid climates leading to such diseases. There may also be dry parasites, which do not manifest as diarrhea but can lead to sores and itching in the lower parts regardless of dry or wet conditions, ultimately becoming fatal if prolonged.

For moisture-related issues resulting in painful diarrhea, boiling medicinal herbs like Huang Lian, Ai Ye, and Ku Shen can be beneficial. If patients have no color around their gums, or a white tongue, experience excessive sleepiness and confusion, or have diarrhea, immediate attention to the lower parts is necessary.

Failure to recognize this will lead to treatments solely affecting the upper regions, neglecting the lower parts where worms may harm the anus, potentially resulting in ulceration that can cause death. Burning moxa in a bamboo tube for fumigation is advised.[37p]

　　　　本事方 【宋　许叔微】

　　　　　治法

　　心虫曰蛔，脾虫曰寸白，肾虫如寸截丝缕，肝虫如烂杏，肺虫如蚕，皆能杀人。惟肺虫为急，居肺叶之内，蚀人肺系，故成瘵疾。由是咳嗽，咯血声嘶，药所不到，治之为难。《道藏经》中载诸虫头皆向下，惟自初一至初五以前，虫头向上，故用药多取效者此也。又姚宽《西溪丛话》云：五脏虫皆上行，唯有肺虫下行，最难治，用獭爪为末调药，于初四初六日治之，此日肺虫上行也。二说小异，姑两存之，以备参考。[38p]

Translation:

On Curing Methods
(From "The Essentials of the Matter" by Xu Shuwei, Song Dynasty)

The heart worm is called "hollow", the spleen worm is known as "cui bai", the kidney worm resembles fine cut threads, the liver worm resembles rotten apricots, and the lung worm is akin to silkworms; all of these can be fatal. Among them, the lung worm is the most urgent, residing within the lung lobes and eroding the lung connections, thus causing tuberculosis. As a result, symptoms include coughing, spitting blood, and a hoarse voice, making treatment challenging as medicine often fails to reach it.

The "Daoist Scriptures" indicate that the heads of all worms point downward, but from the first day to the fifth day of the month, the heads point upward; thus, medications often yield better effects during this period. Additionally, Yao Kuan in "West Creek Miscellaneous Talks" states that all organ worms ascend, but only the lung worm descends, making it particularly difficult to treat. It is advised to grind otter claws into powder to mix with medicine and to treat on the fourth and sixth days, as on these days, the lung worm ascends. The two accounts differ slightly, but both may be retained for reference.[38p]

　　　　证治准绳 【明　王肯堂】

　　　　　九虫

　　虫由湿热郁蒸而生，观之日中有雨，则禾节生虫，其理明矣。善乎张戴人推言之也！曰水火属春夏，湿土属季夏，水从土化，故多虫焉。人患虫积，多由饥饱，调燮失宜，或过餐鱼脍白酒，多食牛羊，或误啖鳖苋，中脘气虚，湿热失运，故生寸白诸虫，或如蚯蚓，或似龟鳖。小儿最多，大人间有。其候心嘈腹痛，呕吐涎沫，面色痿黄，眼眶鼻下青黑，以致饮食少进，肌肉不生，沉沉默默欲眠，微有寒热。如不早治，相生不已。古人云：虫长一尺，则能害人。虫若贯串，杀人甚急。治法追虫取积，以剪红丸、尊神丸、遇仙丹。[39p]

Zheng Zhi Zhun Sheng (Clarifying Treatment Principles) - Ming Dynasty, Wang Kentang

Nine Insects

Insects arise from the accumulation of dampness and heat. Observing that there is rain during the day, one understands that the growth of crops leads to the emergence of insects; this principle is clear. Zhang Dairen aptly expounded on this: water and fire are associated with spring and summer, while damp earth pertains to late summer. Water transforms from the earth, hence there are many insects. Human suffering from insect accumulation primarily arises from imbalances in hunger and satiety, as well as improper regulation. This can happen from excessive consumption of fish, raw meat, and white wine, or mistakenly eating turtles and amaranth, leading to a deficiency in the central qi and disrupted pathway of damp heat, resulting in the emergence of various white worms, which may resemble earthworms or turtles. Children are most commonly affected, but adults can also suffer. Symptoms include heart palpitations, abdominal pain, vomiting frothy saliva, pale and yellowish complexion, dark circles under the eyes and around the nose, leading to reduced food intake, muscle weakness, lethargy, and mild chills or fever. If not treated early, the condition may worsen. The ancients said: if an insect grows to a foot long, it can harm a person. If they multiply rapidly, they can cause urgent harm. Treatment entails removing the insects by addressing the accumulation with remedies such as cutting red pills, Zun Shen pills, or Yu Xian pills.[39p]

　　九虫□□脏腑不实，脾胃皆虚，杂食生冷肥甘油腻盐藏等物，节宣不时，腐败停滞，所以发动。又有神志不舒，精魄失守，及五脏劳热，又病余毒气血积郁而生，或食瓜果与畜兽内脏，遗留诸虫子类而生。虫之为候，呕恶吐涎，口出清沫，痛有去来，乍作乍止。寸白虫色白形褊，损人精气，力乏腰疼。蛲虫细如菜虫，能为痔漏、疮癞、疥癣、痈疽等患。寸白、蛲、蛔，是三者，皆九虫数中之一物也。外此又有儿童疳慝，昏睡烦躁，鼻烂汁臭，齿龂生疮，下利黑血。虫食下部为狐，下唇有疮；虫食其脏为惑，上唇有疮。　　三虫者，谓长虫、赤虫、蛲虫也。[40p]

The nine worms indicate that the organs are unbalanced, with weakness in the spleen and stomach. Consuming mixed foods that are cold, fatty, oily, or salty, and irregular eating habits lead to decay and stagnation, causing disturbances. There may also be a lack of mental clarity, loss of the spirit, and heat in the five organs, along with the accumulation of residual toxins and stagnant blood. Consuming fruits and the internal organs of animals may leave behind certain types of worms. Symptoms of worms include nausea, vomiting foamy saliva, and intermittent pain that comes and goes. The small white worm is white and thin, depleting vital energy, causing weakness and back pain. The pinworm is as fine as a cabbage worm and can lead to conditions like hemorrhoids, sores, skin diseases, and abscesses. The small white worm, pinworm, and roundworm are among the nine types of worms. Additionally, there are children who suffer from malnutrition and restlessness, with rancid nasal discharge and ulcerations in the gums, resulting in dark blood in the stool. Worms affecting the lower part lead to external sores on the lower lip; those affecting the internal organs result in sores on the upper lip. The three worms refer to the long worm, the red worm, and the pinworm.[40p]

乃有九种，而蛲虫及寸白，人多病之。寸白从食牛肉，饮白酒所成，相连一尺则杀人。服药下之，须结裹溃然出尽，乃佳。若断则相生未已，更宜速治之。蛲虫多是小儿患之，大人亦有。其病令人心痛，清朝口吐汁，烦躁则是也。其余各种种不利人，人胃无不有者，宜服九虫丸以除之。　　蛔虫者，是九虫之一也，长一尺，亦有长五六寸。或因脏腑虚弱而动，或因食甘肥而动，其发动则腹中痛发作积聚，行来上下，痛有休息，亦攻心痛，腹中热，口中喜涎及吐清水，贯伤心者则死。诊其脉腹中痛，其脉法当沉弱弦，今反洪而大，则蛔虫也。[41p]

There are nine types of parasitic worms, among which pinworms and ascarids cause many illnesses. Ascarids arise from consuming beef and drinking white wine; a length of one foot can be lethal. When treating with medicine, it is essential for the worms to be expelled completely, so that they come out wrapped together; only then is it effective. If the expulsion is incomplete, the worms will continue to proliferate, thus rapid treatment is necessary. Pinworms often affect children, but adults can also suffer from them. This condition causes heart pain, resulting in the expulsion of bile during a clear morning; agitation is also a symptom. Other types of worms are harmful as well, and since worms are present in everyone’s stomach, it is advisable to take the Nine Worm Pill to eliminate them.

The ascarid is one of these nine worms, typically measuring one foot in length, though some may be five to six inches long. They may become active due to a weakness in the organs or from consuming rich foods. Their activity causes abdominal pain, which can manifest as aggregations that shift up and down, producing intermittent pain. It can also lead to heart pain, heat in the abdomen, an increase in saliva, and the vomiting of clear water; if it severely injures the heart, it can lead to death. When diagnosing, if the pulse indicates abdominal pain, the pulse should ideally be weak and thin, but if it is strong and large, it indicates the presence of ascarids.[41p]

　　蛔蛊，九虫之数，人腹中皆有之。小儿失乳而哺早，或食甜过多，胃虚虫动，令人腹痛恶心，口吐清水，腹上有青筋，火煨史君子与食，以壳煎汤送下，甚妙。然世人多于临卧服之，又无日分，多不验。唯是于月初四五间五更服之，至日午前虫尽下，可以和胃温平药一两日调理之，不可多也。九虫在人腹中，月上旬头向上，中旬横之，下旬头向下，故中下旬用药，即不入虫口，所以不验也。牛马之生子，上旬生者，行在母前；中旬生者，并肩而行；下旬生者，后随之。猫之食鼠亦然，上旬食上段，中旬中段，下旬下段。自然之理，物皆由之，而莫知之。[42p]

The intestinal parasite, known as the "nine worms," exists in everyone’s abdomen. When a young child loses milk too early or consumes too many sweets, it can lead to a weak stomach and the movement of these worms, causing abdominal pain, nausea, and vomiting of clear fluids. If there are visible blue veins on the abdomen, it is effective to prepare the decoction by roasting the historical gentleman and using the shell. However, many people tend to take it before sleeping, without observing the proper timing, and thus do not find it effective. The correct approach is to take it between the fourth and fifth days of the lunar month during the fifth watch, in order to expel the worms completely by noon of that same day. Following this, one may use a warming and balancing medicine for one or two days to regulate the stomach, but not excessively. The nine worms in the abdomen orient themselves according to the lunar phases: in the first ten days of the month, they point upwards; in the middle ten days, they lie horizontally; and in the last ten days, they point downwards. Therefore, medicines taken in the middle or last ten days do not enter the worm's mouth, hence their ineffectiveness. The same principle applies to the offspring of cattle and horses: those born in the first ten days stay ahead of the mother; those born in the middle ten days walk side by side; and those born in the last ten days follow behind. Cats eat mice in a similar manner: they consume the front segment in the first ten days, the middle in the middle ten days, and the rear segment in the last ten days. This is the natural order of things, yet few recognize it.[42p]

　　　　景岳全书 【明　张介宾】

　　　　　论证

　　虫之为病，人多有之，由于化生，诚为莫测。在古方书，虽曰由湿由热，由口腹不节，由食饮停积而生，是固皆有之矣。然以常见验之，则凡脏强气盛者，未闻其有虫，正以随食随化，虫自难存。若夫脏气之弱，行化之迟，所以停聚而渐致生虫耳。然则或由湿热，或由生冷，或由肥甘，或由滞腻，皆可生虫，非独湿热已也。然以数者之中，又惟生冷生虫为最。[43p]

Jing Yue Complete Works
Ming Dynasty - Zhang Jiebin

On Insects' Disease

Insects as a disease are prevalent among many people, stemming from transformation and birth, which is indeed hard to predict. In ancient medical texts, it is said that they arise from dampness, heat, indiscretions in eating and drinking, or the accumulation of food and drink. While these causes certainly exist, from common observations, it is found that those with strong organs and vigorous energy rarely have insects, as their food transforms quickly, making it difficult for insects to survive. Conversely, those with weak organ energy and sluggish transformation tend to have stagnation and consequently develop insects over time. Therefore, insects can arise from damp heat, raw or cold foods, rich and sweet foods, or from clogs and grease; it is not solely damp heat. Nonetheless, among these causes, raw and cold foods are the most likely to produce insects.[43p]

即如收藏诸物，但着生水，或近阴湿，则最易蛀腐，非其义乎？故凡欲爱养小儿，极当节其水果，以防败脾，此实紧要之一端也。至若治虫之法，虽当去虫，而欲治生之之本，以杜其源，犹当温养脾肾元气为主，但使脏气阳强，非惟虫不能留，亦自不能生也。余制有温脏丸方，最所宜也。　　虫之为病，其类不一，或由渐而甚，或由少而多，及其久而为害，则为腹痛食减，渐至羸瘠而危者有之。凡虫痛证，必时作时止，来去无定，或呕吐青黄绿水，或吐出虫，或痛而坐卧不安，或大痛不可忍，面色或青或黄或白，而唇则红。然痛定则能饮食者，便是虫积之证，速宜逐之。[44p]

Just like storing various items, if they are placed in damp conditions or near moisture, they are most easily damaged and rotted; is this not the truth? Therefore, for anyone wanting to care for infants, it is essential to limit their fruit intake to prevent damage to their spleen, which is indeed one of the most crucial points. As for methods to treat parasites, although one should eliminate the parasites, it is equally important to address the underlying cause to prevent their recurrence. One must focus on nurturing the original energy of the spleen and kidneys, ensuring that the internal energy is strong; if this is achieved, not only will the parasites not survive, but they also cannot form in the first place. I have a prescription for warming the internal organs, which is most suitable.

Parasites manifest a variety of ailments; their occurrence may gradually worsen, or increase from few to many. When they become longstanding, they can cause abdominal pain, loss of appetite, and eventually lead to emaciation and danger. Symptoms associated with parasite pain are irregular; they may come and go unpredictably, involve vomiting of greenish-yellow water, or even expulsion of parasites. Pain may lead to restless sitting or lying down, severe pain that is unbearable, and changes in facial complexion, which may appear blue, yellow, or white, while the lips remain red. If the pain settles and the person can still eat and drink, this indicates a buildup of parasites, and it is crucial to expel them promptly.[44p]

　　　　　论治

　　治虫之剂，凡虫势骤急，上攻心腹作痛者，宜扫虫煎，先治其标。若虫积坚固者，宜猎虫丸、遇仙丹、木香槟榔丸、百顺丸之类主之。若稍缓而质弱者，宜荑芜散、化虫散之类主之。丹溪云：打虫方用楝树根、槟榔、鹤虱，夏取汁，冬浓煎饮之。又万应丸最妙。　　治虫之法，按丹溪云：上半月虫头向上易治；下半月虫头向下难治。先以肉汁或糖蜜引虫头向上，然后用药，此皆法之善者。然此乃缓治之法耳。夫虫证甚急，又安能必待其时乎？且以望前望后辨虫头，亦若渺茫无据。惟先用香饵而虫头可引，岂非望后之治亦自有法？又何虑其难治也！　　徐东皋云：治虫之方固多，而用之者不知其法，则亦不能下虫。如丹溪云：虫欲向下之时，必须俟其向上，法当行于月半之前也。[45p]

Discussion on Treatment

Regarding remedies for insects, when the insect's strength is immediate and causes pain in the abdomen, one should use the "Sweep the Insects Decoction" to treat the symptoms first. If the insects are firmly accumulated, one should use pills like "Hunting Insect Pill," "Encounter Immortal Pill," "Wood Fragrance Betel Nut Pill," or "Hundred Smooth Pills" to address the issue. If the condition is somewhat milder and the substance is weaker, remedies like "Epilobium Powder" or "Transform Insect Powder" should be used. Danxi mentions that effective insect treatments use the root of the Chinese toon tree, betel nut, and crane louse, taking the juice in summer and making a strong decoction in winter. Moreover, the "Universal Response Pill" is particularly excellent.

In terms of methods for treating insects, according to Danxi, it's easier to treat when the insect's head is facing upward in the first half of the month; however, it becomes difficult when the head is facing downward in the latter half. One should first draw the insect's head upward with meat juice or syrup, then apply the medicine, as this is a wise strategy. Yet, this is a method for slower treatment. If the insect condition is very urgent, how can one afford to wait for the right timing? Moreover, to distinguish the direction of the insect's head by looking forward and backward is rather vague and lacks evidence. Only by using fragrant bait can one attract the insect's head; is it not true that there is also a method for treating it by looking backward? Why worry about difficulties in treatment?

Xu Donggao states that there are indeed many remedies for treating insects, but those who use them may not understand the methods and thus cannot eliminate the insects. As Danxi said, when insects wish to go downward, one must wait for them to face upward, and the methods should be employed before the middle of the month.[45p]

若虫得食则不食药，亦不能下虫而徒泻其虚也。故虽有方，不知其法，则方亦不效。凡欲下虫，必先一日不食，而使虫饥，次早五更，用油煎肉嚼之，良久，腹内虫闻肉香，头皆向上而欲食，乃以鸡卵煎饼和药嚼而食之，须臾服葱汤或白水，少少以助药力下行，不逾时而虫俱下，甚至数升。然后以白粥补之，随服补剂，调理脾胃，而疾可悉愈。　　一验治法：昔一人患心腹大痛，或止或作，痛不可忍，凡用去积行气等药，百方不效，但于极痛处须用拳捶之，痛得少止，而旋止旋作，久不能愈，日加困弊，莫测其故。忽一胡僧见之曰：予能治也。遂令病者先食香饵，继进一丸，打下一硬嘴异虫，遂愈。此因虫嚙肠脏，所以痛极，捶之则五内震动，虫亦畏而敛伏，不捶则虫得自由，所以复作。此亦验虫奇法。故凡见心腹痛证，但用揉按重捻而痛得暂止者，多有因虫而然也。[46p]

If a worm finds food, it will not eat medicine, nor can it be expelled, leading merely to a drainage of its void. Therefore, even with a prescription, if one does not understand its method, the prescription will be ineffective. Whenever one wishes to expel worms, one must first refrain from eating for a day to make the worms hungry. Then, early at dawn, one should chew meat fried in oil for a long time, so that the worms in the abdomen smell the aroma of the meat, all turning upwards, desiring to eat. Then, take a chicken egg and mix it with the medicine to chew and consume it. Shortly after, drink scallion broth or plain water, a little bit at a time to assist the medicine’s downward action. Without exceeding the time, all the worms will be expelled, sometimes by the volume of several sheng. Then, replenish with plain porridge, continuously taking restorative agents to adjust the spleen and stomach, and the illness can be entirely cured.

An example of this treatment method: Once, a person suffered from severe abdominal pain, sometimes ceasing and sometimes intensifying, unbearable to endure. Although various medicines to remove accumulation and regulate qi were used, none were effective. At the site of the pain, one must strike it with a fist, causing the pain to lessen for a while, but it would soon return, leading to prolonged suffering without understanding the cause. Suddenly, a monk appeared and said: "I can treat this." The patient was then instructed to first eat fragrant bait, followed by a pill, which expelled a strange, hard-mouthed worm, resulting in recovery. This was due to the worm gnawing at the intestines, causing extreme pain; striking it would vibrate the inner organs, making the worm afraid and retreat. If not struck, the worm would roam freely, hence the pain would reoccur. This is verification of the unique method for dealing with worms. Thus, whenever one observes symptoms of abdominal pain, if pressing or kneading temporarily alleviates the pain, it is often due to the presence of worms.[46p]

　　　　　蛔虫

　　凡诸虫之中，惟蛔虫最多，其逐治之法，总若前条。然旋逐旋生，终非善策。欲杜其源，必须温养脾胃，脾胃气强，虫自不生矣。故凡于逐虫之后，或于未逐之先，若欲调补脾胃，则如归脾汤、温胃饮、五君子煎、理中汤或理阴煎之属，皆所宜也。若欲兼虫而治之，则惟温脏丸为最善。凡治虫之法，或攻或补，自有缓急先后之宜，所当详辨，不可任意忽略也。　　巢氏《病源》曰：凡腹中痛，其脉法当沉弱，今脉反洪大，是蛔虫也。
　　　　　寸白虫
[47p]

Roundworm

Among all worms, the roundworm is the most numerous. The methods to expel it are as previously mentioned. However, it can grow back as quickly as it is expelled, which is ultimately not a good strategy. To eliminate it at the source, one must strengthen the spleen and stomach. When the spleen and stomach are strong, the worms will not arise. Therefore, whether after expelling the worms or before, if one wishes to replenish the spleen and stomach, decoctions like Gui Pi Tang, Wen Wei Yin, Wu Jun Zi Jian, Li Zhong Tang, or the remedy for nourishing Yin are suitable. If one seeks to treat the worms at the same time, the best method is the Wen Zang Wan. The methods for treating worms can be either aggressive or nurturing, and one should attend to the appropriate timing and order; careful discernment is necessary and should not be neglected casually. Cao's "Sources of Illness" states: For abdominal pain, if the pulse is sinking and weak, it indicates something else, but if the pulse is surging and large, it signifies roundworms.

Thin White Worm[47p]

　　此虫长寸许，色白，其状如蛆，母子相生，有独行者，有个个相接不断者，故能长至一二丈。治寸白虫无如榧子煎，其效如神。
　　　　　小儿疳虫

　　小儿疳虫，名曰疳(上匿下虫)，亦由饮食过伤，致成疳积，身热腹大，面黄四肢无力，昏睡，鼻烂汁臭，齿龈生疮，或下利黑血，皆腹中有虫故也。宜九味芦荟丸、追虫丸、四味肥儿丸、七味肥儿丸、蟾蜍丸之类主之。虫去之后，仍当调补气血。
　　　　石室秘箓 【清　陈士铎】

　　　　　虫痛

　　虫痛之证，得食则痛减，无食则痛增。以酸梅汤一盏试之，饮下而痛即止，乃虫痛；饮下而痛增重，或少减者，非虫痛也。方用白朮二两，栋树根、白薇各一两，黄连、乌梅肉、吴茱萸炒、栀子、茯苓、甘草、鳖甲各三钱，各为末，蜜为丸，每服三钱，丸如小米大，此丸必须乘其饥饿思食之时与之，此丸服下，必痛甚，不可即与之水，盖虫得水即生也。此方之妙，妙在健脾之中而用杀虫之品。[48p]

This insect is about an inch long, white in color, and resembles maggots. There are those that live alone and those that are connected, which is why they can grow up to one or two zhang (about 3-6 meters). To treat this small white insect, there’s nothing better than frying with nut seeds; its effect is miraculous.

Children's worm ailments

The children's worm ailment, known as "gan" (upper hidden lower worm), is caused by excessive harm from food intake, leading to accumulation of "gan". Symptoms include body heat, a bloated abdomen, a yellowish face, weakness in the limbs, lethargy, a foul-smelling nasal discharge, and sores on the gums. There may be diarrhea with black blood, all due to worms in the abdomen. It is advisable to use formulas such as Nine Flavors Aloe Pill, Chasing Worm Pill, Four Flavor Nourishing Child Pill, Seven Flavor Nourishing Child Pill, and Toad Pills for treatment. After the worms are expelled, one should continue to tonify qi and blood.

Insect pain

The symptom of insect pain is that eating reduces the pain, while not eating increases it. Test with a cup of sour plum soup; if pain stops after drinking, it is insect pain; if drinking increases the pain or only slightly reduces it, then it is not insect pain. The prescription includes two liang of white atractylodes, one liang each of tree root and white smartweed, three qian each of coptis, dried plum core, fried evodia, gardenia, poria, licorice, and turtle shell, all ground to powder and mixed with honey to form pills the size of millet. These should be administered when the person is hungry and craving food. After taking these pills, the pain will surely be intense; do not give them water immediately, as water helps the worms thrive. The brilliance of this formula lies in its ability to strengthen the spleen while using ingredients to kill the worms.[48p]

既是杀虫之药，何故必待其饥饿而始杀之？盖腹中无食则虫不得养，虫口必向上而素食，待其饥饿枵腹之时，则虫头尽向上而不向下矣。一与之食，彼必以为食也，尽来争食之，奈人口拂其性，则乱动而跳跃故转痛甚也。禁与之水，则周身上下耳目口鼻，无非沾染药气，内外夹攻，有死而已。设不知禁忌，仍与之水，虫且借势而翻腾沐浴，药少水多，自然解体，止可杀虫一半，而不能剪草除根矣。故必坚忍须臾一刻之痛，使终身之痛除，愿人忍之哉！大黄亦可加三钱，不加亦可。腹之上疼不宜加，腹之下疼宜加也。[49p]

Since it is a medicine for killing insects, why must we wait until they are hungry to begin the extermination? When there is no food in the stomach, the insects cannot be nourished; their mouths will naturally turn upward to seek food. When they are hungry and empty, their heads will point upward, not downward. If food is given to them, they will certainly think it is food and all rush to compete for it. But when the mouth contradicts their nature, they will stir and jump, causing greater pain. If water is forbidden, then every part of their body—ears, eyes, mouth, and nose—will be contaminated by the medicinal vapor, attacking from within and without, leading only to death. If one does not know this restriction and still gives them water, the insects will take advantage and thrash about, bathing; with more water than medicine, they will naturally break apart, killing only half of them and not uprooting the grass. Therefore, one must endure a moment of pain to eliminate the lifelong suffering. I hope people can endure it! Also, a dose of three qian of rhubarb can be added; it can also be omitted. If there is pain above the abdomen, it is not suitable to increase the dosage; if there is pain below the abdomen, it should be increased.[49p]

Formulae

Gan Cao Xie Xin Decoction: Treats vocal hoarseness due to parasitic infestation in the upper body.
Ingredients: Licorice (4 taels), Huang Qin, Ren Shen, Gan Jiang (3 taels each), Huang Lian (1 tael), Da Zao (12 pieces), Ban Xia (1/2 sheng). Combine the seven ingredients with 10 dou of water, boil to obtain 6 sheng, strain, then re-boil. Administer warm, 1 sheng at a time, three times daily.

Yu Xian Dan: Treats stubborn, hardened parasitic accumulations.
Ingredients: Black coarse head powder, Bingtang (1 jin each), Da Huang (1/2 jin), San Ling, E Zhu (4 taels each, stir-fried), Mu Xiang (2 taels). Grind all to a powder, use Zao Jiao to smash and boil into a concentrated broth, strain, and make into balls the size of a tung seed. Take 4 to 5 pills, adjusted according to strength; consume with clear tea before dawn. If bowel movements are not regular, assist with warm tea. Once the parasites are expelled, replenish with plain rice porridge.

Wu Yi San: Treats severe abdominal pain in adults and children caused by roundworm, or when vomiting greenish-yellow watery phlegm, or expelling worms, with intermittent symptoms; indicated for roundworm-related heart pain.
Ingredients: Wu Yi and Lei Wan (0.5 taels each), Gan Qi (1 tael, crushed and stir-fried until smoke dissipates). Grind all into fine powder, take 3 qian with 7 fen of warm water, no specific timing needed. For severe cases, do not exceed three doses; for children, each dose is 5 fen.[50p]

Wuyisan (Weeds Powder)
Take the following insects: chicken heart betel nut, and three qian each of wuyizhi; one qian of muxiang.
Grind these into a powder to make one dose. First, brew a decoction of sour pomegranate root and wait until the fifth watch of the night to chew the fried meat, directing the insect's head upwards. Then, use the pomegranate root decoction to mix with the medicine and take it warm. The insect will soften and descend. One formula does not include wuyizhi.

Wumei Wan (Black Plum Pills)
Treats cold in the stomach, vomiting of roundworms, and related symptoms. Take thirty pieces of black plum pulp, ginseng, roasted huangbo, xiexin, cinnamon twig, processed fuzi, each six qian; stir-fried huanglian, one liang six qian; dry ginger, one liang; angelica, soaked in wine; and four qian of sichuan pepper, removing seeds and closed mouth parts.
Grind the ingredients into powder, then steam the black plum with wine until soft and mash into a paste. Add honey to form pills the size of a tongzi. Take one to twenty pills each time, three times a day. Avoid raw, cold, and slippery foods. Take with Lizhong Decoction.

Muxiang Binglang Wan (Aromatic Cardamom and Betel Nut Pills)
Treats the preceding symptoms. Take muxiang, green peel with flesh removed, aged tangerine peel with white part removed, stir-fried zhihua, betel nut, and fengzhu, each one liang; skinless huangbo, fried xiangfu, fried dahuang, each three liang; and four liang of black gou, taking the head powder.
Form into pills the size of green peas with water. Take three to fifty pills each time, with ginger soup far from meals, to be taken at a modest dose.[51p]

Hua Chong San (From "Yilin")
Two grains of thunderbolt seed, two pieces of betel nut, one qian of herba centipeda, a little light powder, and seven pieces of shijunzi. Grind the above into a powder, divide into two doses. In the evening, prepare one liang of fresh pork, cut into slices, and soak in soapberry juice overnight. By the fifth watch, roast slowly until cooked, then wipe the meat with fragrant oil. When warm, take one dose of the powder and rub it on the meat, slightly heat it before eating. By the time of the si hour, the worms will be expelled, and then food and drink can be taken.

Gan Chong Fang
For liver worms caused by liver labor, manifesting as fear and unease, with flowers appearing in the eyes. Use three liang of wax tree, three liang of eastward branch, four liang of dry lacquer, and five egg whites. Half a jin of glutinous rice flour. Grind the branch into powder, and decoct with the other ingredients in a copper vessel. Form into small bean-sized pills, and do not eat overnight. In the early morning, take one hundred pills; for children, take fifty pills; the worms will be expelled in decay.

Xin Chong Fang
For heart labor and heat injuring the heart, there exists a long worm named Gu, measuring one foot, causing illness by piercing the heart. Use thunderbolt seed, tangerine peel, peach kernel (or peach skin), five fen each of stone silkworm, six fen of wolf tooth, two pieces of guanzhong, seven fen of Wu zhouyu root and skin, and thirty-seven pieces of stiff silkworm, each four fen of artemisia, blue mallow, and dry lacquer, along with a handful of burnt hair the size of an egg. Grind the twelve ingredients into a powder, form into honey pills the size of a walnut, take seven pills with bitter wine on an empty stomach, gradually increasing up to twenty-seven pills, twice daily. One variation does not include stone silkworm.[52p]

Spleen Worm Formula: Used to treat heat-induced spleen disorders, characterized by white worms in the spleen causing a tendency to vomit out worms.

  • 8 sheng of hemp seed
  • 1 foot of large Wu Yuli root
  • 2 taels of tangerine peel

Mix these three ingredients, chew them, and decoct with water for immediate consumption. When taking, refrain from speaking; if the worms hear the voice, they will not be expelled—this must be strictly avoided.

Lung Worm Formula: Used for lung heat disorders causing worms to develop in the lungs.

  • 1 sheng of mulberry root white bark
  • 5 he of large Wu Zhuyou root white bark
  • 3 taels of wolf tooth

Mix these three ingredients, chew them, and boil with 7 sheng of wine until reduced to 1 sheng, then take it all at dawn.

Kidney Worm Pill: Treats kidney heat disorders, with swollen and urgent limbs, and pinworm-like worms causing disease in the kidneys.

  • 1 tael each of: wild spurge, hu powder, and locust tree bark
  • 40 apricot seeds
  • 2 taels of dry lacquer
  • 3 pieces of guanzhong
  • 50 pieces of Wu Zhuyou

Use these seven ingredients, sieve them together, and take with morning well water, starting with half a spoon and increasing to one and a half spoons until symptoms resolve.

Artemisia Round: Treats minor gastrointestinal infections with tapeworms, resulting in abdominal pain, slight expulsion of white fluid, feelings of anxiety, alternating chills and fever, poor appetite, and emaciation of skin and flesh, accompanied by an inability to lift limbs.

  • 4 fen each of: Qulu and sweet chrysanthemum flower
  • 8 fen each of: artemisia, guanzhong, leicha, shan mei, tian dong, and wolf tooth

Grind these eight ingredients into a powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of soybeans. For a three-year-old, administer five pills; for ages five and older, adjust according to needs, gradually increasing to ten pills.[53p]

　　神效剪红丸　专取一切虫积，神效无比。每于五更鸡鸣时，用冷茶清下，更用马桶盛粪，于野地看之，庶见药功易辨，或虫或积，或如烂鱼冻，或作五色等积。若一次未见虫积，更看第二三次下来，此即是病根。有积消积，有气消气，有虫取虫，有块消块。若病根去，其病自消。若病浅，即一服见效。若源深根固，须再一服，能宣导四时蕴积。春宣积滞，不生疮毒；夏宣暑湿，不生热利；秋宣痰饮，不生瘴疟；冬宣风寒，不生瘟疫。此药温和，不动元阳真气，亦无反恶。小儿半服，孕妇休服。其效如神。　　一、上末，用槟榔生研细，取净末一斤，以二两为母，余十四两，第一次，以一等罗筛过，取齐晒干。　　二、上末，用商陆根，即樟柳根，白者可用，赤者杀人。金毛狗脊、贯众各四两。[54p]

Divine Efficacy Red Pill specially targets all forms of parasitic accumulation, showing unparalleled effectiveness. It should be taken at the break of dawn when the rooster crows, using cold tea for consumption. Additionally, one should collect excrement in a chamber pot and observe it in an open field to easily identify the effects of the medicine, whether it be parasites or accumulated matter, which may resemble rotten fish or various colored accumulations. If no parasites or accumulations are seen after the first attempt, one should check again a second or third time; this indicates the root of the illness. The accumulation will dissolve, the qi will disperse, the parasites will be expelled, and lumps will diminish. If the root of the illness is removed, the ailment will resolve itself. If the condition is mild, a single dose will show results. However, if the source is deeply rooted, a second dose may be necessary, which can clear seasonal accumulations. In spring, it resolves stagnant accumulation, preventing sores and toxins; in summer, it dispels summer heat and dampness, preventing heat-related issues; in autumn, it disperses phlegm and fluids, preventing pestilence; and in winter, it expels wind and cold, preventing epidemics. This medicine is gentle and does not disturb the true qi of the body, nor does it have adverse effects. It is not suitable for children to take fully or for pregnant women to use. Its effects are miraculous.

  1. First, take one pound of finely ground Betel nut powder, using two taels as the base and the remaining fourteen taels to be sifted through a fine sieve for the first time and then dried evenly.

  2. Second, take the root of the zhāngliù (related to the camphor tree), with the white variety being safe to use while the red variety is harmful. Also use four taels each of Jinmao dog spine and Guanzhong.[54p]

已上三味和一处，研极细末，上第二次，以二等罗筛过，取齐晒干。若不用贯众则虫出来犹未死也。　　三、上末用三棱、莪朮并酢煮，各八两。青木香、西木香各四两，雷丸酢煮二两半，南木香二两。已上六味和一处，研极细末，上第三次，以三等罗筛过，取齐。　　四、上末，用大黄銼碎浸酒，晒干研细，取净末一斤，上第四次，以四等罗筛过，取齐晒干。　　五、上末，用黑牵牛半生半炒研细，取头末净一斤，上第五次，以五等罗筛过，取齐晒干。又方，有枳壳一斤为母，有霍香四两和入诸药。　　右作五处另研极细末，要作五次。上末却用茵陈半斤，大皂角一斤，煎汁滤净，法水为丸如菉豆大，晒干后，用丁香末一两，或加芦苍末一两，亦妙。以前净汁煎一滚，洒入丸药，旋摇令光莹为度。再以阿胶二两生，以前汁熬镕洒入丸药，旋摇先莹，晒干。壮人每服五钱，弱人每服四钱，五更以茶清吞下，小儿减半。[55p]

The above three ingredients are to be combined, ground into a very fine powder, and used a second time. Sift through a medium-sized sieve and take the uniform portions for drying. If you do not use the herb Guanzhong, the insects will emerge while still alive.

For the third preparation, take the fine powder and add eight taels each of Sanleng and Ezhucao, four taels each of Qingmuxiang and Ximuxiang, two and a half taels of Leijun vinegar-cooked, and two taels of Nanmuxiang. Combine these six ingredients and grind them into a very fine powder, and for the third time, sift through a fine sieve to collect the uniform portions.

For the fourth preparation, take the fine powder, using Dahuang that has been crushed and soaked in wine, then dried and ground finely. Take one jin of the clean powder, and for the fourth time, sift through a very fine sieve to collect the uniform portions for drying.

For the fifth preparation, take half processed, half roasted Heiqianqiu and grind it finely to yield one jin of the cleaned top powder. For the fifth time, sift through an even finer sieve to collect the uniform portions for drying. Additionally, there is a formula with one jin of Zhike as the main ingredient, and four taels of Huoxiang mixed in with the other medicines.

The methods described above necessitate grinding into a very fine powder, requiring five preparations in total. For these powders, use half a jin of Yinchenshen and one jin of Dazaojiao, decoct to extract the juice and filter clean. Use this liquid to form pills the size of mung beans, then dry. Combine with one tael of clove powder, or add one tael of Lvcang powder for effectiveness. Previously, after simmering the clean juice, sprinkle it over the herbal pills, shaking them to create a glossy finish. Then add two taels of raw Ejiao, melting it in the prior juice and sprinkling it over the pills, shaking them for a glossy finish before drying.

A strong person should take five qian, a weak person four qian, swallowed with clear tea at dawn, and for children, reduce the dose by half.[55p]

　　万应丸　取虫积神效。

Wan Ying Pill is highly effective for expelling parasites.

Take eight taels of black morning glory, rhubarb, and betel nut; one tael each of southern wood fragrance and thunderbolt pill, cooked in vinegar; and five qian of agarwood. Grind the black morning glory, rhubarb, and betel nut together into a powder. Boil four taels each of wild soapberry and neem bark to make a decoction, then form pills the size of mung beans. Finally, coat the pills with a powder made from grinding the thunderbolt pill, wood fragrance, and agarwood together. Take thirty to forty pills each time, swallowed with sugar water around dawn; it can also be taken as a powder.[56p]

　　追虫丸　取一切虫积。
